 is paricharchaa main purv videsh mantri ke natwar singh, varisht patrkaar shekhar gupta, stanbhakaar or videsh niti vishleshak si raja mohan or raajnneetik vigyaani pratap bhanu mehta ne bhi hissaa liya
 Sitapati said that along with the Babri demolition, an attempt was also made to eliminate Rao
 haalanki, shrotaaon main baithe congress netaa manishankar ayyar ne is aarope par kadi aapatti jataai ki unki party ne raav ko khalanaayak ke rup main pesh karne kii koshish kii, taaki muslim vot aakarshith kiye ja saken or is baat par afsos jataayaa ki raav ne masjid ko tode jane se rokane ke liye samay par karrwai nahin kii

 com / pbeezyazb1— Sagar Kabir (@imsagarkabir10)october 5, 2018aapako bataa den ki apane gharelu maidan or apane gharelu darshakon ke saamne duusare din kaa doosraa seshan puri tarah se rabindra jadeja ke naam rahaa
 The star all-rounder of India, batting brilliantly, scored an innings of 100 runs in 132 balls
 is pari ke dauraan rabindra jadeja puri tarah se westeindies ke gendbaajon par akraman karte hue najar aae
 He hit 5 fours and 5 sixes during his innings
 saath hi bharat ko ek bahut bade score tak pahunchaa diya
 Ravindra Jadeja is being praised on Twitter
 ballebaajon ke umdaa pradarshan ke baad tisara perera kii aguai main dhardaar gendbaaji se srilanka ne trikoniya ekadivasiy cricket shrinkhalaa main mangalvaar ko brisben bharat ko aasaani se 51 ran se haraakar ank talika main use antim sthaan par khiskaa diya
 Perera took four wickets for 37 runs to help Team India score 45 despite useful innings of Virat Kohli (66) and Irfan Pathan (47)
 1 over main 238 ran par simat gai
 Kohli also shared a 92-run partnership for the fourth wicket with Suresh Raina (32) but it was not enough to give the team the victory
 nuwan kulshekhara ne perera kaa acha saath nibhaate hue 40 ran par teen wicket chatkaaye jabaki lasith malinga ne do khilaadiyon ko pavilion bheja
 Earlier, Sri Lanka scored 289 for six wickets
 salaami ballebaajon tillakaratne dilashaan (51) or captain mahela jayavardhane (45) ke pehle wicket ke liye 95 ran jodne ke baad lahiru thirimane (62), angelo maithyuj (naabad 49) or dinesh chandimal (38) ne bhi beshkeemtee paariyaan kheli
 The win gave Sri Lanka four points and moved to second place with 11 points from five matches
 bharat chah maichon main 10 ank ke saath antim sthaan par he
 India got off to a poor start in the chase and lost the second ball of Malinga's innings as captain Virender Sehwag (00), who tried to hit a very outside ball off the stump, hit Nuwan on the deep third man
 Caught by Kulasekara
 sachin tendulkar (22) or gautam gambhir (29) acchhee lay main dikhe lekin donon apni galati se wicket ganvaa baithe
 Gambhir also hit two fours in an over from Maharoof but Nuwan Kulasekara was able to play forward and made an easy catch to Perera in the lane
 kohli or raina ne iske baad pari ko aage badhaayaa
 Both were able to add only 15 runs in the five overs of the bowling powerplay taken in the 16th over
 kharaab farm se jujh rahe raina powerple main maithyuj kii pehali hi gend par bhaagyashaalee rahe jab becoward point par dilashaan ne unka kaich chhod diya
 Kohli was also given a score by Chandimal at mid-wicket off Perera and Malinga on 14 and 32 runs, respectively
 kohli or raina ne 23wein over main bharat kaa score 100 ran tak pahunchaaya
 Kohli completed his 20th fifty of his career with the help of a four off 66 balls with a single off the ball from Rangana Herath
 maharuf ne raina ko out karke 92 ran kii is saajhedaari ko todaa
 In an attempt to play Maharuf's ball to the leg side, Raina was caught by Thirimhane on the short cover
 unhone 55 gend kii apni pari main ek chauke kii madad se 32 ran banaae
 India needed 124 runs to win in the last 15 overs
 team ne 36wein over main ballebaaji power play liya
 There was pressure on Kohli to increase the run pace
 unhen perera kii duusari gend ko chaar ran ke liye bheja lekin agali hi gend ko pul karne kii koshish main midaan par kulshekhara ko aasaan kaich de baithe
 Parthiv Patel also became the victim of Perera after scoring four runs
 perera ne aar vinayakumar (00) kii bhi out kiya jabaki ravichandran aswin (05) ko malinga ne pavilion bheja
 Perera got Sri Lanka to victory by dismissing Pathan
 pathan ne 34 gend kii apni pari main saat chauke maare
 Earlier, Sri Lanka got off to bat after winning the toss and the opening pair of Dilshan and Jayawardene gave a fast start
 dilashaan ko aar vinay kumaar ke khilaaf shuruuaat main pareshaani hui lekin baad main unhone karnataka ke is tej gendbaaj par covers main chaukaa jadaa
 Sehwag, playing the role of a captain due to a match ban imposed on regular captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni, handed the ball to Umesh Yadav in the sixth over whose fourth ball was off Dilshan's bat for six runs over the third man while the next ball
 The batsman sent for four runs in covers
 jayavardhane is bich strike rotate karte rahe
 He scored his first four in the eighth over on Yadav and the team also completed 50 runs in the same over
 bharat ko pehali safalataa 19wein over main mili jab pathan kii gend par kaaryvahak captain sahvaag ne farward short leg par ghota lagaate hue jayavardhane kaa behtareen kaich lapka
 He hit two fours in his innings of 55 balls
 bharat ne iske baad donon spinneron aswin or ravindra jadeja ko gendbaaji par lagaaya jinhone ran gati par kuch ankush lagaaya
 Sehwag called Yadav for a second spell in the 28th over and in an attempt to pull his first ball, Kumar Sangakkara (08) was caught by Tendulkar at fine leg
 chandimal or thirimane se iske baad pari ko aage badhaayaa
 Sri Lanka took the power play in the 35th over
 thirimane or chandimal ne 52 gend main ardhashtakeey saajhedaari puri kii
 Pathan broke the 71-run partnership by bowling Chandimal
 iske baad 40wein over main tanaavpurn sthiti ban gai jab aswin gendbaaji ke liye bade lekin thirimane ko krij se baahar dekhakar unhone gilliyaan uda diye
 The comments gendbaaj or sahvaag ne ran out kii apil kii or donon ampire charchaa karne lage
 Tendulkar then persuaded the captain to withdraw the appeal, alleviating tension
 ballebaaji powerple ke paanch over main srilanka ne 30 ran jode jabaki chandimal kaa wicket ganvaaya
 Thirimane completed his half-century in 53 balls with a single off Ashwin
 unhone maithyuj ke saath saat over main 49 ran jode
 Suresh Raina broke the partnership by catching a catch from Thirwin on Ashwin
 maithyuj ne naabad 49 ran kii apni pari ke dauraan 37 gend kaa saamana karte hue chaar chauke or ek chakka jadaa

 Nuwan Kulasekara played well with Perera taking three wickets for 40 runs while Lasith Malinga sent two players to the pavilion
 isse pehle srilanka ne chah wicket par 289 ran banaae
 Lahiru Thirimane (62), Angelo Mathews (49 not out) and Dinesh Chandimal (38) also played valuable innings after opening batsmen Tillakaratne Dilshan (51) and captain Mahela Jayawardene (45) added 95 runs for the first wicket
 is jeet se srilanka ko chaar ank mili or vah paanch maichon main 11 ank ke saath duusare sthaan par pahunch gaya he
 India are in the final spot with 10 points from six matches
 lakshya kaa peechha karne utre bharat kii shuruuaat behad kharaab rahi or usne malinga kii pari kii duusari gend par hi captain virendra sahvaag (00) kaa wicket ganvaa diya jo aaf stump ke behad baahar kii gend par prahaar karne kii koshish main deep third main par nuwan kulshekhara dwaara lapke gaye
 Sachin Tendulkar (22) and Gautam Gambhir (29) looked in good rhythm but both lost wickets due to their mistake
 gambhir ne bhi maharuf ke ek over main do chauke maare lekin nuwan kulshekhara ko aage badhkar khilne kii koshish main gali main perera ko aasaan kaich de baithe
 Kohli and Raina then progressed the innings
 donon 16wein over main liye gayi gendbaaji powerple ke paanch over main keval 15 ran jod paae
 Raina battling poor form, Mathews was lucky on his first ball in the powerplay when Dilshan dropped his catch at backward point
 kohli ko bhi 14 or 32 ran ke score par kramash: perera or malinga kii gend par midwicket par chandimal ne jivadaan diya
 Kohli and Raina reached India's score of 100 runs in the 23rd over
 kohli ne rangana herath kii gend par ek ran ke saath 66 gend main ek chauke kii madad se apane karier kaa 20waan ardhashatak puraa kiya
 Maharuf broke the 92-run partnership by dismissing Raina
 maharuf kii gend ko leg said main khilne kii koshish main raina short cover par thirimane ko kaich de baithe
 He scored 32 runs in his 55-ball knock with the help of a four
 bharat ko antim 15 over main jeet ke liye 124 ran kii darkaar thi
 The team took a batting power play in the 36th over
 kohli par ran gati badhaane kaa dabaav tha
 He was sent by Perera's second ball for four runs but in the attempt to pull the next ball, Kulasekara was caught easy at mid-off
 parthiv patel bhi chaar ran banane ke baad perera kaa shikaar bane
 Perera also dismissed r Vinay Kumar (00) while Malinga sent Ravichandran Ashwin (05) to the pavilion
 perera ne pathan ko out karke srilanka ko jeet dilaayi
 Pathan hit seven fours in his 34-ball innings
 isse pehle tas jitkar ballebaaji karne utre srilanka ko dilashaan or jayavardhane kii salaami jodi ne tej shuruuaat dilaai
 Dilshan had trouble in the beginning against r Vinay Kumar but later he hit the Karnataka fast bowler in the covers
 niyamit captain mahendra singh dhoni par lage ek match ke pratibandh ke kaaran captain kii bhoomika nibhaa rahe sahvaag ne chathe over main gend umesh yadav ko thamai jinaki chauthi gend dilashaan ke balle kaa kinaaraa lekar third main ke upar se chah ran ke liye gai jabaki agali gend ko is ballebaaj ne covers main chaar ran ke liye bheja
 Jayawardene, meanwhile, kept rotating the strike
 unhone apana pehla chaukaa yadav par aathven over main jamaaya or isi over main team ke 50 ran bhi puure hue
 India got their first breakthrough in the 19th over when the caretaker captain Sehwag, off Pathan's ball, dived to a forward short leg, catching Jayawardene's best catch
 unhone 55 gend kii apni pari main do chauke maare
 India then put both spinners Ashwin and Ravindra Jadeja on the bowling who put some control on the run pace
 sahvaag ne 28wein over main yadav ko duusare spel ke liye bulaayaa or unki pehali hi gend ko pul karne kii koshish main kumaar sangakaara (08) fine leg par tendulkar ko kaich thama baithe
 Chandimal and Thirimane then led the innings
 srilanka ne 35wein over main power play liya
 Thirimane and Chandimal completed a half-century partnership in 52 balls
 pathan ne chandimal ko bold karke 71 ran kii is saajhedaari ko todaa
 After this, there was a tense situation in the 40th over when Ashwin went for bowling but seeing Thirimane out of the crease, he blew the balls
 tippaniyan The bowler and Sehwag appealed for a run out and both umpires started discussing
 tendulkar ne iske baad tanaav kam karte hue captain ko apil waapas lene ke liye manaaya
 Sri Lanka added 30 runs in five overs of the batting powerplay while losing Chandimal's wicket

 ab centre sarkaar is grad pranali ko lagu karne ke liye adhisuchana jari karegi or ipisie- enwayament polution control athurity is baat kii nigaraanee karegi ki dilli sarkaar, endiemasi, emsidi or dilli trephic police ne ise kaise lagu kiya
 Under this pollution code, four categories of pollution in Delhi NCR - Poor, Poor, Severe and Severe have been fixed
 gragade system ko chaar bhaagon main baanta gaya he
 1
 Severe or Emergency According to this new grading system if PM2 in the air
 5 kaa str 300 microgram prati cubic meter yaa piem 10 kii maatra agar 500 microgram prati cubic meter ko paar kar jaae or ye sthiti 48 ghante yaa usase zyada ke liye bani rahe to ye upaay kiye jaaen - Entry of diesel trucks to be stopped (other than required items) - nijee vaahanon ke liye od evan yojana shuru kii jaae - Construction activities should be stopped - task force skulon ko band karne samet anya kadam uthaae 2
 Severe category ke tahat PM 2
 These measures should be taken if the quantity of 5 is above 250 micrograms per cubic meter or if PM10 is above 430 micrograms per cubic meter
 
 
 - eenton ke bhatthe band honge - Hot mix plants will be closed - badarpur power plant band hoga - Public transport will be increased - sadakon kii maikenised safai badhaai jaaegi or pani kaa chhidkaav hoga 3
 Very poor - jab PM 2
 5 ranged between 121–250 and PM10 ranged between 351–430
 
 
 - dijal janarator set band honge - Parking fees will be increased by 3-4 times - bas or metro sarvice badhaai jaaegi - The burning of coal and wood in the hotel and open drinking area will be prohibited
 - resident welfare association or colony ke log sardiyon main chaukeedaar ko bijli kaa heater denge - Comments will be alerted to heart patients and other people in TV and newspapers 4
 Moderate to poor category agar PM 2
 If the level of 5 is between 91–120 or the level of PM10 is between 251–350
 
 
 - kooda jalaana band karen - Apply thermal pollution control saath hi supreme court ne yah nirdesh bhi diya he ki centre ensiaar ke kaarkaanon main petro coke or fernes oil ke istemaal kii bhi jaanch kare
 They are used in factories and generators and cause huge amounts of pollution
 centre ko 4 hafte main apni report daakhil kerani hogi
 The court will now hear the next hearing of the case in the second week of January

 PM 2 under Severe category
 5 kii maatra 250 microgram prati cubic meter se upar yaa PM10 agar 430 microgram prati cubic meter se upar ho to ye upaay kiye jaaen
 
 
 - Bricks will be closed - hot mix plant band honge - Badarpur power plant will be closed - public transport ko badhaayaa jayega - Mechanized cleaning of roads will be increased and water sprayed 3
 Very poor - when PM 2
 5 121-250 ke bich main rahe or PM10 351-430 ke bich main ho
 
 
 - Diesel generator sets will be discontinued - parking fees 3-4 guna badhaai jaaegi - Bus and Metro service will be increased - hotel or khule khaane pine vaali jagah main koyale or lakdi ke jalaane par roak hogi - Residents Welfare Association and the people of the colony will give electric heater to the janitor in winter - tivi or akhabaaron main dil ke marijon or duusare logon ko alert karengetippaniyan 4
